module full_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2,
                  input wire cin);
    wire temp1;
    wire temp2;
    wire temp3;
    xor(sum, in1, in2, cin);
    and(temp1,in1,in2);
    and(temp2,in1,cin);
    and(temp3,in2,cin);
    or(cout,temp1,temp2,temp3);
endmodule

module half_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2);
    xor(sum, in1, in2);
    and(cout, in1, in2);
endmodule

module full_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2,
                  input wire cin,
                  );
    wire temp1;
    wire temp2;
    wire temp3;
    xor(sum, in1, in2, cin);
    and(temp1,in1,in2);
    and(temp2,in1,cin);
    and(temp3,in2,cin);
    or(cout,temp1,temp2,temp3);
endmodule

module half_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2);
    xor(sum, in1, in2);
    and(cout, in1, in2);

module half_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2);
    xor(sum, in1, in2);
    and(cout, in1, in2);
endmodule

module full_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2,
                  input wire cin);
    wire temp1;
    wire temp2;
    wire temp3;
    xor(sum, in1, in2, cin);
    and(temp1,in1,in2);
    and(temp2,in1,cin);
    and(temp3,in2,cin);
    or(cout,temp1,temp2,temp3);
endmodule

module half_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2);
    xor(sum, in1, in2);
    and(cout, in1, in2);
endmodule

module full_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2,
                  input wire cin,
                  );
    wire temp1;
    wire temp2;
    wire temp3;
    xor(sum, in1, in2, cin);
    and(temp1,in1,in2);
    and(temp2,in1,cin);
    and(temp3,in2,cin);
    or(cout,temp1,temp2,temp3);
endmodule

module half_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2);
    xor(sum, in1, in2);
    and(cout, in1, in2);
endmodule

module full_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2,
                  input wire cin,
                  );
    wire temp1;
    wire temp2;
    wire temp3;
    xor(sum, in1, in2, cin);
    and(temp1,in1,in2);
    and(temp2,in1,cin);
    and(temp3,in2,cin);
    or(cout,temp1,temp2,temp3);
endmodule

module half_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2);
    xor(sum, in1, in2);
    and(cout, in1, in2);
endmodule

module full_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2,
                  input wire cin,
                  );
    wire temp1;
    wire temp2;
    wire temp3;
    xor(sum, in1, in2, cin);
    and(temp1,in1,in2);
    and(temp2,in1,cin);
    and(temp3,in2,cin);
    or(cout,temp1,temp2,temp3);
endmodule

module half_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2);
    xor(sum, in1, in2);
    and(cout, in1, in2);
endmodule

module full_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2,
                  input wire cin,
                  );
    wire temp1;
    wire temp2;
    wire temp3;
    xor(sum, in1, in2, cin);
    and(temp1,in1,in2);
    and(temp2,in1,cin);
    and(temp3,in2,cin);
    or(cout,temp1,temp2,temp3);
endmodule

//Please finish designing the 8 bit multiplier module (multiplier_8) below.
//There are two 8 bit inputs (A and B) and a 16 bit output (product).
//The module should utilize the inputs (A and B) to determine the output product correctly in its implementation.
module multiplier_8(output [15:0] product, input [7:0] A, B);
 
	wire [7:0] A_B;
	wire [7:0] AB;
	wire [7:0] AB_M;
	wire [7:0] AB_M_1;
	wire [7:0] AB_M_2;
	wire [7:0] AB_M_3;
	wire [7:0] AB_M_4;
	wire [7:0] AB_M_5;
	wire [7:0] AB_M_6;
	wire [7:0] AB_M_7;
	
	assign A_B = A * B;
	assign AB = A * B;
	
	assign AB_M = AB[7:0] << 1;
	assign AB_M_1 = AB_M[7:0] + AB_M[7:0];
	assign AB_M_2 = AB_M_1[7:0] + AB_M_1[7:0];

	assign AB_M_6 = AB_M_5[7:0] + AB_M_5[7:0];

endmodule

//Please finish designing the 8 bit multiplier module (multiplier_8) below.
//There are two 8 bit inputs (A and B) and a 16 bit output (product).
//The module should utilize the inputs (A and B) to determine the output product correctly in its implementation.
module multiplier_8(output [15:0] product, input [7:0] A, B);	
	wire [7:0] A_B;
	wire [7:0] AB;
	wire [7:0] AB_M;
	
	assign A_B = A & B;
	assign AB = A | B;
	
	assign AB_M = AB << 1;
	
	assign product = A_B ^ AB_M;
endmodule

//Please finish designing the 8 bit multiplier module (multiplier_8) below.
//There are two 8 bit inputs (A and B) and a 16 bit output (product).
//The module should utilize the inputs (A and B) to determine the output product correctly in its implementation.
module multiplier_8(output [15:0] product, input [7:0] A, B);

	wire [7:0] AB;

//There are two 8 bit inputs (A and B) and a 16 bit output (product).
//The module should utilize the inputs (A and B) to determine the output product correctly in its implementation.

module half_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2);
    xor(sum, in1, in2);
    and(cout, in1, in2);
endmodule

module full_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2,
                  input wire cin);
    wire temp1;
    wire temp2;
    wire temp3;
    xor(sum, in1, in2, cin);
    and(temp1,in1,in2);
    and(temp2,in1,cin);
    and(temp3,in2,cin);
    or(cout,temp1,temp2,temp3);
endmodule

//Please finish designing the 8 bit multiplier module (multiplier_8) below.
//There are two 8 bit inputs (A and B) and a 16 bit output (product).
//The module should utilize the inputs (A and B) to determine the output product correctly in its implementation.
module multiplier_8(output [15:0] product, input [7:0] A, B);
initial begin
	product = 0;
end
always @(A or B) begin
	product = 0;
	if (A == 0 && B == 0) begin
		product = 0;
	end
	else if (A == 0) begin
		product = {B[7:0], 8'b0};
	end
	else if (B == 0) begin
		product = {A[7:0], 8'b0};
	end
	else begin
		product = A * B;
	end
end
endmodule

//Please finish designing the 8 bit multiplier module (multiplier_8) below.
//There are two 8 bit inputs (A and B) and a 16 bit output (product).
//The module should utilize the inputs (A and B) to determine the output product correctly in its implementation.
module multiplier_8(output [15:0] product, input [7:0] A, B); 
    wire [7:0] pp0, pp1, pp2, pp3, pp4, pp5, pp6, pp7;
    assign pp0 = A[0]? B : 8'b00000000;
    assign pp1 = A[1]? B : 8'b00000000;
    assign pp2 = A[2]? B : 8'b00000000;
    assign pp3 = A[3]? B : 8'b00000000;
    assign pp4 = A[4]? B : 8'b00000000;
    assign pp5 = A[5]? B : 8'b00000000;
    assign pp6 = A[6]? B : 8'b00000000;
    assign pp7 = A[7]? B : 8'b00000000;
    assign product[0] = pp0[0];
    shr_8bit_1 SHR1(product[1], pp0[1], pp1[0]);
    shr_8bit_2 SHR2(product[2], pp0[2], pp1[1], pp2[0]);
    shr_8bit_3 SHR3(product[3], pp0[3], pp1[2], pp2[1], pp3[0]);

//There are two 8 bit inputs (A and B) and a 16 bit output (product).
//The module should utilize the inputs (A and B) to determine the output product correctly in its implementation.
module multiplier_8(output [15:0] product, input [7:0] A, B); 
    wire [7:0] pp0, pp1, pp2, pp3, pp4, pp5, pp6, pp7;
    assign pp0 = A[0]? B : 8'b00000000;
    assign pp1 = A[1]? B : 8'b00000000;
    assign pp2 = A[2]? B : 8'b00000000;
    assign pp3 = A[3]? B : 8'b00000000;
    assign pp4 = A[4]? B : 8'b00000000;
    assign pp5 = A[5]? B : 8'b00000000;
    assign pp6 = A[6]? B : 8'b00000000;
    assign pp7 = A[7]? B : 8'b00000000;
    assign product[0] = pp0[0];
    shr_8bit_1 SHR1(product[1], pp0[1], pp1[0]);
    shr_8bit_2 SHR2(product[2], pp0[2], pp1[1], pp2[0]);
    shr_8bit_3 SHR3(product[3], pp0[3], pp1[2], pp2[1], pp3[0]);
    shr_8bit_4 SHR4(product[4], pp0[4], pp1[3], pp2[2], pp3[1], pp4[0]);

    shr_8bit_6 SHR6(product[6], pp0[6], pp1[5], pp2[4], pp3[3], pp4[2], pp5[1], pp6[0]);
    shr_8bit_7 SHR7(product[7], pp0[7], pp1[6], pp2[5], pp3[4], pp4[3], pp5[2], pp6[1], pp7[0]);
endmodule

module shr_8bit_1(output reg [7:0] product, input [7:0] A, input B);
    always @(A or B)
    begin
        if(B[0])
            product <= A;
        else
            product <= 8'b00000000;
    end
endmodule

    shr_8bit_1 SHR1(product[1], pp0[1], pp1[0]);
    shr_8bit_2 SHR2(product[2], pp0[2], pp1[1], pp2[0]);
    shr_8bit_3 SHR3(product[3], pp0[3], pp1[2], pp2[1], pp3[0]);
    shr_8bit_4 SHR4(product[4], pp0[4], pp1[3], pp2[2], pp3[1], pp4[0]);
    shr_8bit_5 SHR5(product[5], pp0[5], pp1[4], pp2[3], pp3[2], pp4[1], pp5[0]);
    shr_8bit_6 SHR6(product[6], pp0[6], pp1[5], pp2[4], pp3[3], pp4[2], pp5[1], pp6[0]);
    shr_8bit_7 SHR7(product[7], pp0[7], pp1[6], pp2[5], pp3[4], pp4[3], pp5[2], pp6[1], pp7[0]);
endmodule

module shr_8bit_1(output reg [7:0] product, input [7:0] A, input B);
    always @(A or B)
    begin
        if(B[0])
            product <= A;
        else
            product <= 8'b00000000;
    end
endmodule

        else
            product <= 8'b00000000;
    end
endmodule

wire [7:0] product_temp;

reg [7:0] product_temp_2;
reg [7:0] product_temp_3;

end

//Please finish designing the 8 bit multiplier module (multiplier_8) below.
//There are two 8 bit inputs (A and B) and a 16 bit output (product).
//The module should utilize the inputs (A and B) to determine the output product correctly in its implementation.
module multiplier_8(output [15:0] product, input [7:0] A, B);
localparam zero = 0;
localparam one = 1;
always @(A or B)
begin
	case(A)
		zero:
		begin
			case(B)
				zero:
					product = zero;
				one:
					product = zero;
				default:
					product = zero;
			endcase
		end
		one:
		begin
			case(B)

					product = one;
				one:
					product = one;
				default:
					product = one;
			endcase
		end
		default:
			product = zero;
	endcase
end
endmodule

module half_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2);
    xor(sum, in1, in2);
    and(cout, in1, in2);
endmodule

module full_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2,
                  input wire cin,
                  );
    wire temp1;
    wire temp2;
    wire temp3;
    xor(sum, in1, in2, cin);
    and(temp1,in1,in2);
    and(temp2,in1,cin);
    and(temp3,in2,cin);
    or(cout,temp1,temp2,temp3);
endmodule

module full_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2,
                  input wire cin);
    wire temp1;
    wire temp2;
    wire temp3;
    xor(sum, in1, in2, cin);
    and(temp1,in1,in2);
    and(temp2,in1,cin);
    and(temp3,in2,cin);
    or(cout,temp1,temp2,temp3);
endmodule

    full_adder FA3(s3, c4, pp0[5], pp1[4], pp2[3], c3);
    full_adder FA4(s4, c5, pp0[6], pp1[5], pp2[4], c4);
    full_adder FA5(s5, c6, pp0[7], pp1[6], pp2[5], c5);
    full_adder FA6(s6, c7, pp1[7], pp2[6], pp3[5], c6);
    half_adder HA7(s7, c8, pp2[7], pp3[6]);
    
    assign product[7] = s7;
    assign product[8] = s6;
    assign product[9] = s5;
    assign product[10] = s4;
    assign product[11] = s3;
    assign product[12] = s2;
    assign product[13] = s1;
    assign product[14] = s0;
    assign product[15] = pp7[7];
endmodule

module half_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2);
    xor(sum, in1, in2);
    and(cout, in1, in2);
endmodule

module full_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2,
                  input wire cin,
                  );
    wire temp1;
    wire temp2;
    wire temp3;
    xor(sum, in1, in2, cin);
    and(temp1,in1,in2);
    and(temp2,in1,cin);
    and(temp3,in2,cin);
    or(cout,temp1,temp2,temp3);
endmodule

module half_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2);
    xor(sum, in1, in2);
    and(cout, in1, in2);
endmodule

module full_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2,
                  input wire cin,
                  );
    wire temp1;
    wire temp2;
    wire temp3;
    xor(sum, in1, in2, cin);
    and(temp1,in1,in2);
    and(temp2,in1,cin);
    and(temp3,in2,cin);
    or(cout,temp1,temp2,temp3);
endmodule

module multiplier_16(output [15:0] product, input [15:0] A, B);

	wire [15:0] AB;
	
	assign A_B = A & B;
	assign AB = A_B << 1;
	
	wire [15:0] product_temp;
	
	multiplier_8 M1(product_temp, A_B, AB);
	
	assign product = product_temp;
	
endmodule

module half_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2);
    xor(sum, in1, in2);
    and(cout, in1, in2);
endmodule

module full_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2,
                  input wire cin,
                  );
    wire temp1;
    wire temp2;
    wire temp3;
    xor(sum, in1, in2, cin);
    and(temp1,in1,in2);
    and(temp2,in1,cin);
    and(temp3,in2,cin);
    or(cout,temp1,temp2,temp3);
endmodule

module half_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2);
    xor(sum, in1, in2);
    and(cout, in1, in2);
endmodule

module full_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2,
                  input wire cin,
                  );
    wire temp1;
    wire temp2;
    wire temp3;
    xor(sum, in1, in2, cin);
    and(temp1,in1,in2);
    and(temp2,in1,cin);
    and(temp3,in2,cin);
    or(cout,temp1,temp2,temp3);
endmodule

//Please finish designing the 8 bit multiplier module (multiplier_8) below.
//There are two 8 bit inputs (A and B) and a 16 bit output (product).
//The module should utilize the inputs (A and B) to determine the output product correctly in its implementation.
module multiplier_8(output [15:0] product, input [7:0] A, B);										
	wire [7:0] A_B;
	wire [7:0] AB;
	wire [7:0] AB_M;
	
	assign A_B = A & B;
	assign AB = A | B;
	
	assign AB_M = AB << 1;
	
	wire [7:0] product_1;
	wire [7:0] product_2;
	
	multiplier_4 M1(product_1, A_B, AB_M);
	multiplier_4 M2(product_2, A, AB);
	
	assign product = product_1 | product_2;
	
endmodule

module full_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2,
                  input wire cin,
                  );
    wire temp1;
    wire temp2;
    wire temp3;
    xor(sum, in1, in2, cin);
    and(temp1,in1,in2);
    and(temp2,in1,cin);
    and(temp3,in2,cin);
    or(cout,temp1,temp2,temp3);
endmodule

module half_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2);
    xor(sum, in1, in2);
    and(cout, in1, in2);
endmodule

module full_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2,
                  input wire cin,
                  );
    wire temp1;
    wire temp2;
    wire temp3;
    xor(sum, in1, in2, cin);
    and(temp1,in1,in2);
    and(temp2,in1,cin);
    and(temp3,in2,cin);
    or(cout,temp1,temp2,temp3);
endmodule

module half_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2);
    xor(sum, in1, in2);
    and(cout, in1, in2);
endmodule

module full_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2,
                  input wire cin,
                  );
    wire temp1;
    wire temp2;
    wire temp3;
    xor(sum, in1, in2, cin);
    and(temp1,in1,in2);
    and(temp2,in1,cin);
    and(temp3,in2,cin);
    or(cout,temp1,temp2,temp3);
endmodule

                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2);

endmodule

module full_adder(output wire sum,
                  output wire cout,
                  input wire in1,
                  input wire in2,
                  input wire cin,
                  );
    wire temp1;
    wire temp2;
    wire temp3;
    xor(sum, in1, in2, cin);
    and(temp1,in1,in2);
    and(temp2,in1,cin);
    and(temp3,in2,cin);
    or(cout,temp1,temp2,temp3);
endmodule

//Please finish designing the 8 bit multiplier module (multiplier_8) below.
//There are two 8 bit inputs (A and B) and a 16 bit output (product).
//The module should utilize the inputs (A and B) to determine the output product correctly in its implementation.
module multiplier_8(output [15:0] product, input [7:0] A, B);				   
	wire [7:0] A_B;
	wire [7:0] AB;
	wire [7:0] AB_M;
	
	assign A_B = A & B;
	assign AB = A | B;
	
	assign AB_M = AB << 1;
	
	assign product = A_B ^ AB_M;
endmodule
